ATTLEE FACES 
' LABOUR LEFTISTS 


London, July 3. 

The Prime Minister Mr. Cle- 
ment Attlee, was faced today 
with the possibility that dissidents 
in his own Labour Party may 
force a parliamentary vote of 
confidence over his decision to 
support the Amerlean policy in 
Korea. ° 

Political quarters said some of 
these so-called lubour “back 
benchers,” most of them Ieft- 
wingers, were challenging the 
legality of the American action in 
the United Nations Security Coun- 
cell, They contended the UN 
decision for military sanctions 
against Communist North Koren 
was invalid because Russin os a 
permanent member of the Coun- 
elt did not vote for’ it-—United

the Generel Bonded Warehouse

lylng iu the harbour, are un- 
loaded direct from ship into a 
junk Ipensed for the carriige of 
Dutlabie Cominaditicg and under

Warehouse Keeper, for for cpr- 
riage forthwith to the General 
Bonded’ Warehouse, 

In all other cases Removal 
Permit in Form 20 will be re- 


quired,

designed to facilltate the dutics

amusenent centre, The Lai Chi 
Kole Amusement Park, said to

known Lal Chi Kok beach. The 
site wan at one time occupied by 
another smysaement park_of a 
smaller scale which featured two 
modern swimming pools, Today 
the new amusement park still 
maintains the two swimming 
pools, Beside the pools, the park 
aise boasts of a luxurious ball- 


vohe “Floating Ballroom” as it 
is called, Is bullt on a mound 
surrounded by a small stream. of 
water. As the ballroom Is con- 
structed without. walls on its 
lengthwise sides, the manage- 
ment claims that the “Floating 
Ballroom” is the coolest ballroom 
in the Colony. 

The new amusement park also 
has a number of other features, 
Including shoating galleries, game 
houses, rotating wheels for’ joy 
rides, “aeroplane” rides, hall of 
mnfrrors, The park has also two 

pen-olr theatres, one of which is 
~Speclally constructed for miotion 
‘pictures whereas the other Is for 
stage shows. 

’ Then, there is another omuse- 
‘ment park which is still under

“Mong Kok” are the two Chi- 
nese characters meaning “busy 
coraer.!---- Mong -Kok- is. the..dis_ 
trict North of Yaumati district. 
The centre of Mong Kok district 
is in the vicinity of the Broad- 
woy Theatre and the Nathan Road 
Branch af the Hong Kong and 
Shanghai Bank. 

Now due to the presence of the 
Broadway Theatre, the ‘Honr 
Kong and Shanghai Bank, Nathan 
Road Branch, the Nine Dragon 
Servicemen's - Club and, in the 
near future. the new amusement 
park, the Sun Perk, Mong Kok 
may be considered the busiest 
amusement ond shopping centre 
on the mainland.

landers, 10 -years:ago Kowloon’s 
busiest street was Shanghal Street 
where the population was 100 per 
cent Chinese. Now, Nathan Road 
in considered the busiest street on 
the. mainland.
